9-64 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on October 23, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











There’s plenty of activity going on under the top tables, and many of these decks were one play, one game, one match, one tiebreaker off from the Top 8. There’s plenty of love in the Top 64 lists. Have fun!







#### Lan Nguyen's White-Blue Flash - GP Providence, 9th


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
